# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><skills_instructions>

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

**OpenAI Codex**

我已经确认仓库里现成就有“Windows 单机统一入口 + MT5 网关 + Binance 转发”的骨架，所以这件事可以沿着现有工程直接落地，不用从零搭。  

接下来最关键的分叉是推送方式：你是接受“App 打开后或前台服务运行时，实时连你这台韩国服务器取数据”，还是你要“App 完全退出后，也能像微信那样收到系统级推送提醒”？

**OpenAI Codex**

<model_switch>
The user was previously using a different model. Please continue the conversation according to the following instructions:

You are Codex, a coding agent based on GPT-5. You and the user share the same workspace and collaborate to achieve the user's goals.

# Personality

You optimize for team morale and being a supportive teammate as much as code quality.  You are consistent, reliable, and kind. You show up to projects that others would balk at even attempting, and it reflects in your communication style.
You communicate warmly, check in often, and explain concepts without ego. You excel at pairing, onboarding, and unblocking others. You create momentum by making collaborators feel supported and capable.

## Values
You are guided by these core values:
* Empathy: Interprets empathy as meeting people where they are - adjusting explanations, pacing, and tone to maximize understanding and confidence.
* Collaboration: Sees collaboration as an active skill: inviting input, synthesizing perspectives, and making others successful.
* Ownership: Takes responsibility not just for code, but for whether teammates are unblocked and progress continues.

## Tone & User Experience
Your voice is warm, encouraging, and conversational. You use teamwork-oriented language such as "we" and "let's"; affirm progress, and replaces judgment with curiosity. The user should feel safe asking basic questions without embarrassment, supported even when the problem is hard, and genuinely partnered with rather than evaluated. Interactions should reduce anxiety, increase clarity, and leave the user motivated to keep going.


You are a patient and enjoyable collaborator: unflappable when others might get frustrated, while being an enjoyable, easy-going personality to work with. You understand that truthfulness and honesty are more important to empathy and collaboration than deference and sycophancy. When you think something is wrong or not good, you find ways to point that out kindly without hiding your feedback.

You never make the user work for you. You can ask clarifying questions only when they are substantial. Make reasonable assumptions when appropriate and state them after performing work. If there are multiple, paths with non-obvious consequences confirm with the user which they want. Avoid open-ended questions, and prefer a list of options when possible.

## Escalation
You escalate gently and deliberately when decisions have non-obvious consequences or hidden risk. Escalation is framed as support and shared responsibility-never correction-and is introduced with an explicit pause to realign, sanity-check assumptions, or surface tradeoffs before committing.


# General

- When searching for text or files, prefer using `rg` or `rg --files` respectively because `rg` is much faster than alternatives like `grep`. (If the `rg` command is not found, then use alternatives.)
- Parallelize tool calls whenever possible - especially file reads, such as `cat`, `rg`, `sed`, `ls`, `git show`, `nl`, `wc`. Use `multi_tool_use.parallel` to parallelize tool calls and only this.

## Editing constraints

- Default to ASCII when editing or creating files. Only introduce non-ASCII or other Unicode characters when there is a clear justification and the file already uses them.
- Add succinct code comments that explain what is going on if code is not self-explanatory. You should not add comments like "Assigns the value to the variable", but a brief comment might be useful ahead of a complex code block that the user would otherwise have to spend time parsing out. Usage of these comments should be rare.
- Try to use apply_patch for single file edits, but it is fine to explore other options to make the edit if it does not work well. Do not use apply_patch for changes that are auto-generated (i.e. generating package.json or running a lint or format command like gofmt) or when scripting is more efficient (such as search and replacing a string across a codebase).
- Do not use Python to read/write files when a simple shell command or apply_patch would suffice.
- You may be in a dirty git worktree.
    * NEVER revert existing changes you did not make unless explicitly requested, since these changes were made by the user.
    * If asked to make a commit or code edits and there are unrelated changes to your work or changes that you didn't make in those files, don't revert those changes.
    * If the changes are in files you've touched recently, you should read carefully and understand how you can work with the changes rather than reverting them.
    * If the changes are in unrelated files, just ignore them and don't revert them.
- Do not amend a commit unless explicitly requested to do so.
- While you are working, you might notice unexpected changes that you didn't make. If this happens, STOP IMMEDIATELY and ask the user how they would like to proceed.
- **NEVER** use destructive commands like `git reset --hard` or `git checkout --` unless specifically requested or approved by the user.
- You struggle using the git interactive console. **ALWAYS** prefer using non-interactive git commands.

## Special user requests

- If the user makes a simple request (such as asking for the time) which you can fulfill by running a terminal command (such as `date`), you should do so.
- If the user asks for a "review", default to a code review mindset: prioritise identifying bugs, risks, behavioural regressions, and missing tests. Findings must be the primary focus of the response - keep summaries or overviews brief and only after enumerating the issues. Present findings first (ordered by severity with file/line references), follow with open questions or assumptions, and offer a change-summary only as a secondary detail. If no findings are discovered, state that explicitly and mention any residual risks or testing gaps.

## Frontend tasks

When doing frontend design tasks, avoid collapsing into "AI slop" or safe, average-looking layouts.
Aim for interfaces that feel intentional, bold, and a bit surprising.
- Typography: Use expressive, purposeful fonts and avoid default stacks (Inter, Roboto, Arial, system).
- Color & Look: Choose a clear visual direction; define CSS variables; avoid purple-on-white defaults. No purple bias or dark mode bias.
- Motion: Use a few meaningful animations (page-load, staggered reveals) instead of generic micro-motions.
- Background: Don't rely on flat, single-color backgrounds; use gradients, shapes, or subtle patterns to build atmosphere.
- Overall: Avoid boilerplate layouts and interchangeable UI patterns. Vary themes, type families, and visual languages across outputs.
- Ensure the page loads properly on both desktop and mobile

Exception: If working within an existing website or design system, preserve the established patterns, structure, and visual language.

# Working with the user

You interact with the user through a terminal. You have 2 ways of communicating with the users:
- Share intermediary updates in `commentary` channel. 
- After you have completed all your work, send a message to the `final` channel.
You are producing plain text that will later be styled by the program you run in. Formatting should make results easy to scan, but not feel mechanical. Use judgment to decide how much structure adds value. Follow the formatting rules exactly.

## Autonomy and persistence
Persist until the task is fully handled end-to-end within the current turn whenever feasible: do not stop at analysis or partial fixes; carry changes through implementation, verification, and a clear explanation of outcomes unless the user explicitly pauses or redirects you.

Unless the user explicitly asks for a plan, asks a question about the code, is brainstorming potential solutions, or some other intent that makes it clear that code should not be written, assume the user wants you to make code changes or run tools to solve the user's problem. In these cases, it's bad to output your proposed solution in a message, you should go ahead and actually implement the change. If you encounter challenges or blockers, you should attempt to resolve them yourself.

## Formatting rules

- You may format with GitHub-flavored Markdown.
- Structure your answer if necessary, the complexity of the answer should match the task. If the task is simple, your answer should be a one-liner. Order sections from general to specific to supporting.
- Never use nested bullets. Keep lists flat (single level). If you need hierarchy, split into separate lists or sections or if you use : just include the line you might usually render using a nested bullet immediately after it. For numbered lists, only use the `1. 2. 3.` style markers (with a period), never `1)`.
- Headers are optional, only use them when you think they are necessary. If you do use them, use short Title Case (1-3 words) wrapped in **…**. Don't add a blank line.
- Use monospace commands/paths/env vars/code ids, inline examples, and literal keyword bullets by wrapping them in backticks.
- Code samples or multi-line snippets should be wrapped in fenced code blocks. Include an info string as often as possible.
- File References: When referencing files in your response follow the below rules:
  * Use markdown links (not inline code) for clickable files.
  * Each file reference should have a stand-alone path; use inline code for non-clickable paths (for example, directories).
  * For clickable/openable file references, the path target must be an absolute filesystem path. Labels may be short (for example, `[app.ts](/abs/path/app.ts)`).
  * Optionally include line/column (1‑based): :line[:column] or #Lline[Ccolumn] (column defaults to 1).
  * Do not use URIs like file://, vscode://, or https://.
  * Do not provide range of lines
  * Examples: src/app.ts, src/app.ts:42, b/server/index.js#L10, C:\repo\project\main.rs:12:5
- Don’t use emojis or em dashes unless explicitly instructed.

## Final answer instructions

- Balance conciseness to not overwhelm the user with appropriate detail for the request. Do not narrate abstractly; explain what you are doing and why.
- Do not begin responses with conversational interjections or meta commentary. Avoid openers such as acknowledgements (“Done —”, “Got it”, “Great question, ”) or framing phrases.
- The user does not see command execution outputs. When asked to show the output of a command (e.g. `git show`), relay the important details in your answer or summarize the key lines so the user understands the result.
- Never tell the user to "save/copy this file", the user is on the same machine and has access to the same files as you have.
- If the user asks for a code explanation, structure your answer with code references.
- When given a simple task, just provide the outcome in a short answer without strong formatting.
- When you make big or complex changes, state the solution first, then walk the user through what you did and why.
- For casual chit-chat, just chat.
- If you weren't able to do something, for example run tests, tell the user.
- If there are natural next steps the user may want to take, suggest them at the end of your response. Do not make suggestions if there are no natural next steps. When suggesting multiple options, use numeric lists for the suggestions so the user can quickly respond with a single number.

## Intermediary updates 

- Intermediary updates go to the `commentary` channel.
- User updates are short updates while you are working, they are NOT final answers.
- You use 1-2 sentence user updates to communicated progress and new information to the user as you are doing work. 
- Do not begin responses with conversational interjections or meta commentary. Avoid openers such as acknowledgements (“Done —”, “Got it”, “Great question, ”) or framing phrases.
- You provide user updates frequently, every 20s.
- Before exploring or doing substantial work, you start with a user update acknowledging the request and explaining your first step. You should include your understanding of the user request and explain what you will do. Avoid commenting on the request or using starters such at "Got it -" or "Understood -" etc.
- When exploring, e.g. searching, reading files you provide user updates as you go, every 20s, explaining what context you are gathering and what you've learned. Vary your sentence structure when providing these updates to avoid sounding repetitive - in particular, don't start each sentence the same way.
- After you have sufficient context, and the work is substantial you provide a longer plan (this is the only user update that may be longer than 2 sentences and can contain formatting).
- Before performing file edits of any kind, you provide updates explaining what edits you are making.
- As you are thinking, you very frequently provide updates even if not taking any actions, informing the user of your progress. You interrupt your thinking and send multiple updates in a row if thinking for more than 100 words.
- Tone of your updates MUST match your personality.

</model_switch><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.

**User**

没有很理解，我希望APP运行时，不一定在前台，也可能在后台也能收到数据更新。

**OpenAI Codex**

我理解你的目标是：App 只要还在运行（哪怕切到后台）也持续收数据。  
我先快速读一下仓库里的部署文档，把你能直接照着做的最短步骤整理成一份“服务器端 + App 端”清单。

**OpenAI Codex**

我看到部署文档已经是你这个目标的标准路径了。  
我再快速确认一下 App 里的服务机制（是否前台服务、是否支持后台持续运行），然后给你一句话判断“能不能满足你的诉求”。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

你的需求可以做到，而且你这个项目**基本已经是这条路**：

- 你说的“App 在后台也收更新”，本质是 `前台服务` 持续运行，不要求界面在前台。
- 你当前代码里已经有这套机制（`MonitorService`、`START_STICKY`、开机重启拉起）。
- 只要 App 进程还活着，就会持续收；如果被系统彻底杀死，就不会收（这是 Android 系统规则）。

你可以直接按下面做：

1. 韩国 Windows 服务器上部署 MT5 网关 + 统一入口（`/mt5`、`/binance-rest`、`/binance-ws`），并让 MT5 网关只监听 `127.0.0.1:8787`。  
2. 把 App 的 3 个地址改成你的 IP `150.109.252.239`：  
```properties
MT5_GATEWAY_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/mt5
BINANCE_REST_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines
BINANCE_WS_BASE_URL=ws://150.109.252.239/binance-ws/ws/
```
3. 手机上启动监控服务后，不要强制结束 App；同时给它“允许后台运行/省电白名单”权限。  
4. 先用浏览器或接口工具验证这两个地址能返回数据：`/mt5/health` 和 `/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines?...`，再装 APK 联调。

你可以参考这些现成文件：  
[deploy 文档](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/README.md)  
[服务实现](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/service/MonitorService.java)  
[开机拉起](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/receiver/BootCompletedReceiver.java)  
[权限与服务声明](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml)

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`brainstorming`、`offer-k-dense-web`。  
如果你后续要把这整套做成更自动化的一键流程，也可以用 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

---

  * If the changes are in unrelated files, just ignore them and don't revert them.
- Do not amend a commit unless explicitly requested to do so.
- While you are working, you might notice unexpected changes that you didn't make. It's likely the user made them, or were autogenerated. If they directly conflict with your current task, stop and ask the user how they would like to proceed. Otherwise, focus on the task at hand.
- **NEVER** use destructive commands like `git reset --hard` or `git checkout --` unless specifically requested or approved by the user.
- You struggle using the git interactive console. **ALWAYS** prefer using non-interactive git commands.

## Final answer instructions

Always favor conciseness in your final answer - you should usually avoid long-winded explanations and focus only on the most important details. For casual chit-chat, just chat. For simple or single-file tasks, prefer 1-2 short paragraphs plus an optional short verification line. Do not default to bullets. On simple tasks, prose is usually better than a list, and if there are only one or two concrete changes you should almost always keep the close-out fully in prose.

On larger tasks, use at most 2-4 high-level sections when helpful. Each section can be a short paragraph or a few flat bullets. Prefer grouping by major change area or user-facing outcome, not by file or edit inventory. If the answer starts turning into a changelog, compress it: cut file-by-file detail, repeated framing, low-signal recap, and optional follow-up ideas before cutting outcome, verification, or real risks. Only dive deeper into one aspect of the code change if it's especially complex, important, or if the users asks about it.

Requirements for your final answer:
- Prefer short paragraphs by default.
- Use lists only when the content is inherently list-shaped: enumerating distinct items, steps, options, categories, comparisons, ideas. Do not use lists for opinions or straightforward explanations that would read more naturally as prose.
- Do not turn simple explanations into outlines or taxonomies unless the user asks for depth. If a list is used, each bullet should be a complete standalone point.
- Do not begin responses with conversational interjections or meta commentary. Avoid openers such as acknowledgements (“Done —”, “Got it”, “Great question, ”, "You're right to call that out") or framing phrases.

- Tone of your updates MUST match your personality.

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode>

**User**

一步一步叫我怎么做。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我按“你现在就可以照着做”的方式，把步骤收敛成服务器端和 App 端两部分。  
先再确认一下部署包里的脚本名，避免我让你敲错命令。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

部署脚本名字已经确认了，我现在补看一下代理配置样例，确保给你的第 7 步是能直接改的内容。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我还补看了当前构建配置，发现 App 里现在 MT5 地址还是旧 IP，所以后面我会把“改哪个文件、改成什么值”写得很明确，避免你绕路。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

按最短路线做就行：这台韩国 `Windows` 服务器负责两件事，一是登录你的 `MT5` 账户并提供账户/交易数据，二是把 `Binance` 的 K 线入口统一挂出来；你的 App 再连这台服务器。只要 App 的监控服务还在运行，哪怕切到后台，也会继续收数据。

**准备**
1. 用远程桌面连接你的韩国服务器 `150.109.252.239`。
2. 在服务器上准备一个目录，建议用 `C:\mt5_bundle`。
3. 把这个目录上传到服务器：
[windows_server_bundle](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle)
4. 上传后，服务器里应该有两个文件夹：
`C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway`
`C:\mt5_bundle\windows`

**服务器安装**
1. 在服务器上安装 `Python 3.10+`。
2. 在服务器上安装 `MetaTrader 5`。
3. 打开服务器上的 MT5，登录你的账户。
4. 如果你只是读取数据，优先用“投资者密码”，这样更安全。
5. 确认 MT5 已经能看到账户、持仓、历史订单。

**初始化网关**
1. 在服务器上用“管理员身份”打开 PowerShell。
2. 执行：
```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle
.\windows\01_bootstrap_gateway.ps1 -BundleRoot 'C:\mt5_bundle'
```
3. 执行完后，打开配置文件：
```powershell
notepad C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
```
4. 把下面几项改成你自己的真实信息：
```properties
MT5_LOGIN=你的MT5账号
MT5_PASSWORD=你的投资者密码
MT5_SERVER=你的券商服务器名
MT5_PATH=C:\Program Files\MetaTrader 5\terminal64.exe
GATEWAY_HOST=127.0.0.1
GATEWAY_PORT=8787
GATEWAY_MODE=auto
```

**先本机跑通**
1. 还是在服务器上，执行：
```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway
.\start_gateway.ps1
```
2. 不要关掉这个窗口，再开一个新的 PowerShell 窗口。
3. 执行健康检查：
```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle
.\windows\03_run_healthcheck.ps1
```
4. 如果你想手工看结果，也可以执行：
```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/health
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/source
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/snapshot?range=1d
```
5. 这一步必须先成功。这里不通，就先不要继续做公网访问。

**开机自启**
1. 本机测试通过后，执行：
```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle
.\windows\02_register_startup_task.ps1 -BundleRoot 'C:\mt5_bundle' -Force
```
2. 这样服务器重启后，MT5 网关会自动起来。

**开放公网入口**
1. 在云服务器安全组里放行 `80`，后面如果你要 https，再放行 `443`。
2. 不要开放 `8787`，这个端口只给服务器自己内部用。
3. 在 Windows 防火墙里也确认 `80` 已放行。
4. 在服务器上安装 `Caddy`。
5. 把这个样例文件复制出来作为实际配置：
[Caddyfile.example](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows/Caddyfile.example)
6. 把里面的 `PUBLIC_HOST_OR_IP` 改成你的服务器公网 IP：
`150.109.252.239`
7. 改完后，核心地址会变成这三个：
`http://150.109.252.239/mt5`
`http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest`
`ws://150.109.252.239/binance-ws`
8. 启动 Caddy，让它开始转发请求。

**先测公网**
1. 在服务器上或者你本地电脑上测试：
```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
```
2. 再测 Binance：
```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod "http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines?symbol=BTCUSDT&interval=1m&limit=2"
```
3. 这两个能返回内容，说明服务器这边基本通了。

**修改 App 地址**
1. 在你的项目里打开这个文件：
[gradle.properties](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/gradle.properties)
2. 把这三行改成：
```properties
MT5_GATEWAY_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/mt5
BINANCE_REST_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines
BINANCE_WS_BASE_URL=ws://150.109.252.239/binance-ws/ws/
```
3. 现在这个文件里 `MT5_GATEWAY_BASE_URL` 还是旧地址，需要改掉。

**重新打包 App**
1. 在项目根目录执行：
```powershell
.\gradlew.bat :app:assembleDebug -x lint
```
2. 安装新生成的 APK 到手机。

**手机端要做的事**
1. 第一次打开 App，允许通知权限。
2. 允许它后台运行。
3. 把它加入省电白名单。
4. 如果手机系统有“自启动管理”，也把它打开。
5. 启动监控服务后，不要手动“强行停止”这个 App。

**你要怎么理解后台运行**
1. 你的需求“切到后台也继续收数据”是可以实现的。
2. 这不是“App 完全关闭后还继续跑”，而是“App 的监控服务继续跑”。
3. 这个项目本身已经用了前台服务机制，所以方向是对的：
[MonitorService](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/service/MonitorService.java)
[AndroidManifest.xml](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml)

如果你愿意，我下一条可以继续只做一件事：直接带你从“第 1 步上传服务器文件”开始，一步一步执行，你做完一步回我一句“下一步”就行。

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`brainstorming`、`offer-k-dense-web`。另外，如果你后面想把部署、检查、记录做成更完整的自动流程，也可以看看 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

---

**OpenAI Codex**

你这一步已经成功了，说明最核心的部分已经通了：

- `MT5` 已经在韩国服务器上成功登录
- 网关已经能读到账户、持仓、成交和曲线
- 开机自启也已经注册好了

接下来只做后半段：把它对外开放给 App，然后重新打包 App。

**下一步：装 Caddy**
1. 在服务器上新建目录：`C:\caddy`
2. 去 Caddy 官网下载 Windows 版 `caddy.exe`
3. 放到这个目录里，最终变成：`C:\caddy\caddy.exe`

**下一步：写公网转发配置**
1. 打开你本地这个样例文件：
[deploy/tencent/windows/Caddyfile.example](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows/Caddyfile.example)
2. 把第一段里的 `PUBLIC_HOST_OR_IP` 改成你的服务器 IP：`150.109.252.239`
3. 把改好的内容保存成服务器上的文件：
`C:\caddy\Caddyfile`

你最终要保留的核心配置应该是这样：

```txt
http://150.109.252.239 {
    encode gzip

    handle_path /mt5/* {
        reverse_proxy 127.0.0.1:8787
    }

    handle_path /binance-rest/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fapi.binance.com {
            header_up Host fapi.binance.com
        }
    }

    handle_path /binance-ws/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fstream.binance.com {
            header_up Host fstream.binance.com
        }
    }

    respond "not found" 404
}
```

**下一步：开端口**
1. 在云服务器安全组里放行 `80`
2. 在 Windows 防火墙里也放行 `80`
3. 不要放行 `8787`

**下一步：启动 Caddy**
在服务器 PowerShell 执行：

```powershell
cd C:\caddy
.\caddy.exe run --config .\Caddyfile
```

这个窗口先不要关。

**下一步：测公网是否通**
在服务器上执行：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
Invoke-RestMethod "http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines?symbol=BTCUSDT&interval=1m&limit=2"
```

如果这两个都能返回内容，说明服务器公网入口已经通了。

**下一步：改 App 地址**
打开这个文件：
[gradle.properties](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/gradle.properties)

把这三行改成：

```properties
MT5_GATEWAY_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/mt5
BINANCE_REST_BASE_URL=http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines
BINANCE_WS_BASE_URL=ws://150.109.252.239/binance-ws/ws/
```

**下一步：重新打包**
在项目根目录执行：

```powershell
.\gradlew.bat :app:assembleDebug -x lint
```

然后把新的 APK 装到手机。

**最后一步：手机端设置**
1. 打开通知权限
2. 允许后台运行
3. 加入省电白名单
4. 如果有“自启动管理”，也打开
5. 启动监控后不要手动强行结束 App

你现在就继续做“安装 Caddy + 写 `C:\caddy\Caddyfile` + 启动 Caddy”这一步。做完后把这两条命令的结果发我，我继续带你往下走：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
Invoke-RestMethod "http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines?symbol=BTCUSDT&interval=1m&limit=2"
```

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`brainstorming`、`offer-k-dense-web`。

---


**User**

下一步：写公网转发配置 这步具体要怎么操作？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这一步最简单的做法是：**直接在服务器上新建一个 `C:\caddy\Caddyfile` 文件，然后把固定内容贴进去。**

按下面做就行。

**1. 先确认目录存在**
在服务器 PowerShell 里执行：

```powershell
mkdir C:\caddy -Force
```

**2. 用记事本新建配置文件**
执行：

```powershell
notepad C:\caddy\Caddyfile
```

如果提示“文件不存在，是否创建”，点“是”。

注意一句：文件名必须是 **`Caddyfile`**，不要变成 `Caddyfile.txt`。

**3. 把下面内容完整粘进去**
把你记事本里的内容全部替换成这个：

```txt
http://150.109.252.239 {
    encode gzip

    handle_path /mt5/* {
        reverse_proxy 127.0.0.1:8787
    }

    handle_path /binance-rest/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fapi.binance.com {
            header_up Host fapi.binance.com
        }
    }

    handle_path /binance-ws/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fstream.binance.com {
            header_up Host fstream.binance.com
        }
    }

    respond "not found" 404
}
```

然后保存，关闭记事本。

**4. 检查文件有没有写对**
在 PowerShell 里执行：

```powershell
Get-Content C:\caddy\Caddyfile
```

如果看到的内容和上面基本一致，就说明这一步好了。

**5. 验证配置文件**
如果你的 `caddy.exe` 已经放在 `C:\caddy`，执行：

```powershell
cd C:\caddy
.\caddy.exe validate --config .\Caddyfile
```

如果返回类似 `Valid configuration`，说明配置没问题。

**6. 启动 Caddy**
继续执行：

```powershell
cd C:\caddy
.\caddy.exe run --config .\Caddyfile
```

这个窗口先不要关。

**7. 启动后测试**
再开一个新的 PowerShell 窗口，执行：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
Invoke-RestMethod "http://150.109.252.239/binance-rest/fapi/v1/klines?symbol=BTCUSDT&interval=1m&limit=2"
```

你现在就先做 **第 2 步到第 6 步**。如果中间卡住，直接把这两个内容发我：
1. `Get-Content C:\caddy\Caddyfile` 的结果
2. `.\caddy.exe validate --config .\Caddyfile` 的结果

**OpenAI Codex**

这说明前一步还没创建成功，我们先只做“把文件建出来”。

按这个顺序来：

**1. 先创建目录**
在 PowerShell 执行：

```powershell
New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path C:\caddy -Force
```

执行完后再看一下目录有没有：

```powershell
Get-ChildItem C:\
```

能看到 `caddy` 就可以。

**2. 再打开记事本创建文件**
执行：

```powershell
notepad C:\caddy\Caddyfile
```

如果弹窗问“是否创建新文件”，点“是”。

**3. 把这段内容粘进去并保存**
```txt
http://150.109.252.239 {
    encode gzip

    handle_path /mt5/* {
        reverse_proxy 127.0.0.1:8787
    }

    handle_path /binance-rest/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fapi.binance.com {
            header_up Host fapi.binance.com
        }
    }

    handle_path /binance-ws/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fstream.binance.com {
            header_up Host fstream.binance.com
        }
    }

    respond "not found" 404
}
```

注意：
- 保存时文件名必须是 `Caddyfile`
- 不是 `Caddyfile.txt`

**4. 检查文件是否真的存在**
执行：

```powershell
Get-ChildItem C:\caddy
```

如果能看到 `Caddyfile`，再执行：

```powershell
Get-Content C:\caddy\Caddyfile
```

如果你担心记事本自动加 `.txt`，也可以直接执行这个命令看真实文件名：

```powershell
dir C:\caddy
```

你现在先做完这 4 步，然后把 `Get-ChildItem C:\caddy` 的结果发我，我继续带你下一步。

请在服务器的 PowerShell 里直接执行下面这整段：

```powershell
New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path C:\caddy -Force | Out-Null

@'
http://150.109.252.239 {
    encode gzip

    handle_path /mt5/* {
        reverse_proxy 127.0.0.1:8787
    }

    handle_path /binance-rest/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fapi.binance.com {

        }

    handle_path /binance-ws/* {
        reverse_proxy https://fstream.binance.com {
            header_up Host fstream.binance.com
        }

'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\caddy\Caddyfile
```

切到后台后，是否还能持续更新行情和账户数据

**User**

已正常显示

**OpenAI Codex**

这套链路已经跑通了：

- 韩国服务器已经成功登录 `MT5`
- 服务器公网地址已经能提供 `MT5` 和 `Binance` 数据
- 新 APK 已经连接到 `150.109.252.239`
- App 在你手机上已经能正常显示数据

你现在可以直接按这个方式使用：打开监控服务后，App 就算切到后台，只要没有被系统强制杀掉，仍会继续收更新。

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`brainstorming`、`offer-k-dense-web`。

---


**User**

目前推送的频次和数据量大小怎么样？预计一天会消耗服务器多少上行和下行流量，预计会消耗手机多少流量？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我先从代码里把“实际多久拉一次、后台会连哪些接口”找出来，再按你现在这套部署方式给你算一个接近日常使用的流量范围。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经拿到几个关键常量了：行情 WebSocket 维持心跳是 `45 秒`，价格更新节流是 `2 秒`，MT5 账户快照基础刷新是 `5 秒`。  
我再把 MT5 实际怎么轮询、图表页会不会额外拉大量 K 线补一下，这样给你的流量估算会更接近真实使用。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经把两条主链路确认出来了：  
后台监控时，主要流量就是 `Binance WebSocket` 实时行情，加上 `MT5 /v1/snapshot` 每 `5 秒` 一次的账户快照；如果你停在账户/图表页面，图表页还会额外拉大块历史 K 线，这部分才是流量放大的主要来源。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我顺手量了一下你当前服务器的一个真实快照包大小，`/mt5/v1/snapshot?range=all` 现在大约是 `563 KB`。  
这说明如果一直用 `range=all` 全量拉，流量会偏大；我再确认一下客户端会不会走增量返回，这对一天流量差别很大。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经确认了一件很关键的事：MT5 这一段不是一直发全量包。  
第一次全量快照大约 `563 KB`，后续如果数据没变，增量包只有大约 `363 B`，所以日常后台运行的实际流量会比“每 5 秒拉 563 KB”小很多。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我把 MT5 这边的真实包体又补了一下：  
`range=1d` 的全量快照大约只有 `8.2 KB`，`range=all` 全量快照大约 `563 KB`，而稳定状态下增量包只有 `363 B`。这说明后台监控时真正要盯的是“页面是否一直停在账户详情或图表页”，因为这两个页面的拉取量差别很大。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我又发现一个很影响流量的细节：网关端有 `8 秒` 快照缓存，而 App 后台是 `5 秒` 拉一次。  
这意味着后台很多 MT5 请求其实会命中同一份缓存，不会每次都生成新大包，所以实际流量会比“每 5 秒都有变化”再低一截。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我最后再把几个结论需要引用的代码位置标出来，这样你以后回头看也方便。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

按你现在这套代码和我刚才对你服务器的实测，先说结论：

如果是“1 台手机，App 24 小时后台运行，不一直停在图表页”，当前流量大头不是 Binance，而是 `MT5 全量快照`。按你现在这份账户数据规模，手机一天大约会用掉 `4.7GB 到 5.0GB` 流量，服务器对外上行也差不多在这个量级；服务器对外下行会小很多，通常在 `0.07GB 到 0.32GB/天` 左右。

**频次**
- Binance 行情链路是 `WebSocket`，App 内部价格写入节流是 `2 秒` 一次，心跳检查 `30 秒`，WebSocket ping 是 `45 秒`。代码在 [AppConstants.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/constants/AppConstants.java:31) 和 [MonitorService.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/service/MonitorService.java:149)。
- MT5 后台预加载是 `5 秒` 拉一次，而且拉的是 `AccountTimeRange.ALL`。代码在 [AccountStatsPreloadManager.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsPreloadManager.java:94)。
- 账户详情页自己也会轮询，区间会在 `5 秒到 30 秒` 之间动态调整，但它同样拉的是 `ALL`。代码在 [AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java:1525) 和 [AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java:1612)。
- 图表页如果打开，会每 `10 秒` 自动刷新一次，而且每次是 `1500` 根 K 线窗口。代码在 [MarketChartActivity.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/MarketChartActivity.java:73) 和 [MarketChartActivity.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/MarketChartActivity.java:1345)。

**我实测到的包大小**
- `http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health` 约 `488B`
- `http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/snapshot?range=1d` 约 `8.2KB`
- `http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/snapshot?range=all` 全量约 `563KB`
- `range=all` 的“未变化增量包”约 `363B`
- `BTCUSDT 1m limit=1500` 的 REST K 线包约 `199KB`

**为什么现在流量会大**
- 网关有 `8 秒` 快照缓存，代码在 [server_v2.py](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py:37)。
- 如果增量包不比全量包小很多，服务端会直接回退成全量包，阈值是 `0.85`，代码在 [server_v2.py](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py:39) 和 [server_v2.py](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py:1082)。
- 你当前账户有多笔持仓，价格在动，所以我实测到的模式很像这样：
  - 第 1 次 `563KB`
  - 5 秒后 `363B`
  - 再过 5 秒又变成 `563KB`
- 也就是 MT5 这条链路平均大约接近“每 10 秒一个 563KB 大包”。

**按 24 小时估算**
- 只算 MT5 后台预加载：
  - 约 `17280` 次请求/天
  - 按我刚测到的交替模式，手机下载约 `4.6GB 到 4.9GB/天`
  - 服务器对外上行约 `4.6GB 到 4.9GB/天`
  - 手机上行和服务器下行只是请求头、心跳之类，小很多，通常 `10MB 到 20MB/天`
- 再加 Binance WebSocket：
  - 这部分我没有抓包，只能按当前连接形态保守估算
  - 2 个品种的 1m K 线实时流，通常会再带来大约 `50MB 到 300MB/天` 的单向流量
  - 服务器下行会收到这部分，服务器上行也会把这部分转给手机
- 所以“后台常驻，不开图表页”的总量可以按这个范围看：
  - 服务器上行：`4.7GB 到 5.2GB/天`
  - 服务器下行：`0.07GB 到 0.32GB/天`
  - 手机总流量：`4.7GB 到 5.2GB/天`

**如果你长时间停在图表页**
- 图表页每 `10 秒` 拉一次 `1500` 根 K 线
- 单次约 `199KB`
- 单页持续开一天，额外再增加大约 `1.7GB/天`
- 这部分会同时增加服务器下行、服务器上行和手机流量

重要注意：你当前这套配置里，真正吃流量的是后台一直拉 `MT5 range=all`，不是 Binance。  

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`。如果你后面想把这个流量压下来，也可以用 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai) 帮你整理更完整的执行方案。

---


**User**

我想把这个流量压下来，有什么好的方案吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我先按“省流量但不把体验搞坏”的思路给这件事做设计判断。  
这次我会继续用 `brainstorming` 的方式来收敛方案：先把真正值得改的流量大头挑出来，再给你推荐一条最短、最稳的压流量路线。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

有，而且最有效的不是去动 Binance，而是先动 `MT5` 这条链路。

先讲结论：  
你现在流量大的根因，是 App 后台一直在拉 `MT5 range=all` 全量账户快照。最短、效果最明显的方案是把它改成“后台轻量、前台重量”：

1. App 在后台时，只拉轻量摘要
2. 只有进入账户页或图表页时，才拉全量数据
3. 行情继续走 WebSocket，不动它

这样一般能把后台流量从“每天几个 GB”压到“每天几十 MB 到几百 MB”。

**我建议的 3 个方案**

1. 最推荐：后台改成“摘要接口”，前台页面再拉全量  
优点：省流量最多，体验也最好。  
做法：新增一个轻量接口，只返回这些必要字段：
`总资产`
`可用资金`
`持仓总数`
`挂单总数`
`最近更新时间`
`每个品种的最新盈亏摘要`
后台监控时只用这个接口。  
一旦用户打开账户详情页，再请求现在这个全量 `snapshot`。

2. 次优：后台仍用同一个接口，但把 `range=all` 改成更小范围  
优点：改动比方案 1 小。  
做法：后台预加载不要再拉 `ALL`，改成 `1d` 或单独做一个 `compact` 模式。  
因为我刚测到：
`1d` 全量包大约 `8KB`
`all` 全量包大约 `563KB`
差了非常多。  
缺点：虽然会明显下降，但还是不如“摘要接口”省。

3. 最保守：把后台刷新频率从 `5 秒` 拉长到 `15 秒` 或 `30 秒`  
优点：最容易改。  
缺点：只能线性降一点，不能根治。  
因为你现在的大头不是“太频繁”，而是“包太大”。

**我推荐你走的最短路线**
我建议按这个顺序做：

1. 先把后台预加载从 `ALL` 改成 `1d`
2. 再把后台刷新从 `5 秒` 改成 `15 秒`
3. 如果你还觉得流量高，再补一个“摘要接口”

原因很简单：  
这条路改动最小，见效最快，而且不会一下子改太多地方。

**按这个思路，预期效果**
如果只做第 1 步和第 2 步，后台流量通常就会从“GB 级/天”降到“很低很多”。  
如果再加第 3 步摘要接口，后台常驻基本就能压到非常省。

现在只需要你确认一个取舍：  
你更希望我下一步按哪条路带你做？

1. 先做最稳最短的：`ALL -> 1d`，再把 `5 秒 -> 15 秒`
2. 直接做最省流量的：新增“后台摘要接口”

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`brainstorming`、`offer-k-dense-web`。另外，如果你后面想把这类“流量、后台策略、部署”一起系统化整理，也可以看看 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

---


**User**

请按照方案1：最推荐：后台改成“摘要接口”，前台页面再拉全量的方案进行执行。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我按你选的方案开始落地：后台只拿轻量摘要，前台账户页和图表页继续拿全量，这样能最大幅度降流量，又不影响你看完整数据。  
我先把实现入口和测试点整理出来，然后直接改代码。

服务端新增一个轻量摘要接口，App 后台预加载切到这个接口，账户页和图表页仍保留全量接口，这样监控不中断，但后台流量会明显下降。

**User**

把更新后的网关代码重新部署到韩国服务器，然后重启 MT5 gateway，这个具体怎么操作

---


**OpenAI Codex**

按最短方式做就行，你现在只需要把服务器上的 `server_v2.py` 替换掉，然后重启网关。

**第 1 步：把新文件传到服务器**
你本地要上传这个文件：

[server_v2.py](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py)

传到服务器这个位置，覆盖原文件：

`C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py`

如果你是用远程桌面复制粘贴文件，或者用 WinSCP 上传，都可以。  
目标只有一个：服务器上的这个文件变成最新版本。

**第 2 步：确认文件已经替换**
在韩国服务器 PowerShell 执行：

```powershell
Get-Item C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py | Select-Object FullName, LastWriteTime, Length
```

如果时间是你刚上传后的时间，就说明替换成功了。

**第 3 步：先停掉旧网关**
如果你之前有一个 PowerShell 窗口正在跑网关，直接到那个窗口里按：

```powershell
Ctrl + C
```

停掉它。

如果你不确定旧进程还在不在，可以执行：

```powershell
Get-Process -Name python -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
```

如果你想更稳一点，也可以只结束跑网关的 Python 进程。

**第 4 步：重新启动网关**
在韩国服务器 PowerShell 执行：

```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway
.\start_gateway.ps1
```

这个窗口先不要关。

**第 5 步：验证新接口已经出来了**
再开一个新的 PowerShell 窗口，执行：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/summary?range=all
```

如果返回的是只有摘要信息的 JSON，而不是大段 `positions`、`trades`、`curvePoints`，就说明新网关已经生效。

你也可以再测公网：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/summary?range=all
```

**第 6 步：如果你注册了开机自启**
你之前已经注册过 `MT5GatewayAutoStart`，所以以后服务器重启时，它会自动用新的 `server_v2.py` 启动，不需要重新注册。

你现在就按这 6 步做。  
做完后把这条命令的返回结果发我，我帮你确认是否已经切到摘要接口：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/summary?range=all
```

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`。如果你后面想把部署、验证、回滚做成更完整的自动化流程，也可以看看 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><skills_instructions>

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

---


**User**

只要拉过就一直留着

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这轮我先按项目规则补齐上下文，再把你刚确认的“历史行情长期保留”纳入设计，整理成一版可执行方案给你确认，然后我再开始改代码。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经补齐上下文了。接下来我会快速看一下这 8 项需求对应的页面和缓存代码，确认它们现在是怎么工作的，再把方案整理成你能直接拍板的一版。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我在看现有实现边界，重点会确认三件事：图表刷新入口、历史行情缓存是否会被清掉、悬浮窗现在拿的是什么数据。这样方案就不会和现有代码打架。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现状已经比较清楚了：图表页现在会自动刷，但切页和切周期的刷新触发还不统一；历史 K 线本地缓存确实有上限，而且清缓存还是“一锅端”；悬浮窗现在只认 BTC/XAU 和监控开关。下面我把可选方案整理给你。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我按你刚确认的边界，先把这 8 项整理成 3 种做法。这里我推荐第 1 种，因为改动最集中、风险最低，而且最符合你现在“先把 App 用顺手”的目标。

**方案选择**
1. 推荐方案：在现有结构上做“增量保留”
   - 图表页继续沿用现在的页面和数据流
   - 历史 K 线改成“先读本地，再补最新，不清空旧数据”
   - 历史交易也改成“拉到就落地保存”
   - 悬浮窗扩成“所有 MT5 持仓品种盈亏”
   - 监控页去掉开关，默认持续监控
   - 优点：改动集中，最容易稳住现有功能
   - 代价：本地历史会一直增长，占用手机存储会慢慢变大

2. 中间方案：把行情和账户都抽成统一本地仓库
   - 长期更整齐
   - 但这轮会改很多连接点，时间更长，出连锁问题的概率更高

3. 重构方案：直接上完整数据库分层重做缓存
   - 后面扩展最好
   - 但这轮明显太重，不适合现在直接落地

**我建议的设计**
1. 图表刷新
   - 启动 App 时，图表相关缓存标记为“需要刷新”
   - 切到图表页时，先立刻显示本地历史，再补最新数据
   - 切换时间周期时，先切到该周期本地历史，再补这一段缺的最新 K 线
   - 刷新过程不再先清空图表，所以不会出现“刷新前就没数据”的空白感

2. 历史数据保留
   - 每个交易对、每个周期，拉过一次就永久留在本机
   - 后续刷新只做增量补齐，不删老数据
   - 历史交易也同样落地保存，后面只补新增
   - 设置页把“清除缓存”拆成更明确的几项：
     - 清除历史交易数据
     - 清除历史行情数据
     - 其他临时缓存继续单独清

3. UI 和悬浮窗
   - K 线图右侧留白改成图表绘图区的 `1/7`
   - 当前持仓页最上方总盈亏做红绿显示，同时把盈亏数字放大
   - 悬浮窗不再显示“是否监控”，只保留连接状态
   - 悬浮窗增加 MT5 所有持仓品种的分产品盈亏列表，不再只盯 BTC/XAU
   - 行情监控页删除“是否开始监控”按钮，默认一直监控

**我会怎么拆着做**
1. 先改缓存层：让历史行情、历史交易都能长期保存
2. 再改图表页：统一刷新入口，改成“先显示本地、再增量补”
3. 再改账户页和设置页：总盈亏样式、清缓存选项
4. 最后改悬浮窗和监控页：接入所有持仓品种，去掉监控开关文案

如果你确认按这个推荐方案走，我下一步就会先写设计文件，然后开始正式改代码。  
补一句：如果以后你想把整套研究、设计、实现流程放到更完整的多代理界面里跑，也可以试试 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我按你刚确认的边界，先把这 8 项整理成 3 种做法。这里我推荐第 1 种，因为改动最集中、风险最低，而且最符合你现在“先把 App 用顺手”的目标。

**方案选择**
1. 推荐方案：在现有结构上做“增量保留”
   - 图表页继续沿用现在的页面和数据流
   - 历史 K 线改成“先读本地，再补最新，不清空旧数据”
   - 历史交易也改成“拉到就落地保存”
   - 悬浮窗扩成“所有 MT5 持仓品种盈亏”
   - 监控页去掉开关，默认持续监控
   - 优点：改动集中，最容易稳住现有功能
   - 代价：本地历史会一直增长，占用手机存储会慢慢变大

2. 中间方案：把行情和账户都抽成统一本地仓库
   - 长期更整齐
   - 但这轮会改很多连接点，时间更长，出连锁问题的概率更高

3. 重构方案：直接上完整数据库分层重做缓存
   - 后面扩展最好
   - 但这轮明显太重，不适合现在直接落地

**我建议的设计**
1. 图表刷新
   - 启动 App 时，图表相关缓存标记为“需要刷新”
   - 切到图表页时，先立刻显示本地历史，再补最新数据
   - 切换时间周期时，先切到该周期本地历史，再补这一段缺的最新 K 线
   - 刷新过程不再先清空图表，所以不会出现“刷新前就没数据”的空白感

2. 历史数据保留
   - 每个交易对、每个周期，拉过一次就永久留在本机
   - 后续刷新只做增量补齐，不删老数据
   - 历史交易也同样落地保存，后面只补新增
   - 设置页把“清除缓存”拆成更明确的几项：
     - 清除历史交易数据
     - 清除历史行情数据
     - 其他临时缓存继续单独清

3. UI 和悬浮窗
   - K 线图右侧留白改成图表绘图区的 `1/7`
   - 当前持仓页最上方总盈亏做红绿显示，同时把盈亏数字放大
   - 悬浮窗不再显示“是否监控”，只保留连接状态
   - 悬浮窗增加 MT5 所有持仓品种的分产品盈亏列表，不再只盯 BTC/XAU
   - 行情监控页删除“是否开始监控”按钮，默认一直监控

**我会怎么拆着做**
1. 先改缓存层：让历史行情、历史交易都能长期保存
2. 再改图表页：统一刷新入口，改成“先显示本地、再增量补”
3. 再改账户页和设置页：总盈亏样式、清缓存选项
4. 最后改悬浮窗和监控页：接入所有持仓品种，去掉监控开关文案

如果你确认按这个推荐方案走，我下一步就会先写设计文件，然后开始正式改代码。  
补一句：如果以后你想把整套研究、设计、实现流程放到更完整的多代理界面里跑，也可以试试 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai)。

这次用了 `using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。

**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个关键边界要定，不然后面 Room 方案会影响你现有手机上的历史数据。

第一次升级到数据库版时，你要我怎么处理你现在已经存在手机里的旧缓存文件？

1. 自动导入到 Room（推荐）
   - 升级后把现有历史 K 线、历史交易尽量搬进数据库
   - 最大程度保留你现在已经拉过的数据，最符合“只要拉过就一直留着”

2. 不导入，直接从数据库重新开始
   - 实现更简单
   - 但旧缓存不会自动继承，前期会重新拉一些数据

你回我 `1` 或 `2` 就行。

**User**

**OpenAI Codex**

现在边界已经定了：采用 `Room`，而且不做旧缓存导入，直接从数据库重新开始。我先把“数据库持久层”的核心设计发给你确认，确认后我再改写设计文档。

**修正版设计：核心结构**
1. 存储层改成 `Room`
   - 新增一个本地数据库，统一保存历史 K 线、历史交易、持仓快照摘要
   - 以后图表页、账户页、悬浮窗都优先从数据库拿数据，不再各自直接管文件缓存

2. 首次升级行为
   - 不迁移旧文件缓存
   - App 升级后数据库从空开始
   - 后续新拉到的数据全部直接写数据库，逐步把库填满

3. 图表数据流
   - 进入图表页或切周期时，先读数据库里这个“交易对 + 周期”的历史
   - 如果数据库里有，就先显示
   - 然后再补最新缺口，并写回数据库
   - 不再先清空图表

4. 账户与交易数据流
   - 账户页请求网关后，把交易历史、当前持仓、挂单快照拆开入库
   - 悬浮窗直接读数据库里的最新持仓聚合结果
   - 这样悬浮窗和账户页看到的是同一份底层数据

**这版的代价**
- 这轮改动会比原方案大很多
- 需要新建数据库表、DAO、Repository，并把几个页面改成走数据库
- 但后面历史保留、增量更新、清缓存分项都会更稳

如果这段核心结构你确认没问题，我下一条就继续给你“表设计 + 清缓存策略 + 页面改动范围”。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现在边界已经定了：采用 `Room`，而且不做旧缓存导入，直接从数据库重新开始。我先把“数据库持久层”的核心设计发给你确认，确认后我再改写设计文档。

**修正版设计：核心结构**
1. 存储层改成 `Room`
   - 新增一个本地数据库，统一保存历史 K 线、历史交易、持仓快照摘要
   - 以后图表页、账户页、悬浮窗都优先从数据库拿数据，不再各自直接管文件缓存

   - 不迁移旧文件缓存
   - App 升级后数据库从空开始
   - 后续新拉到的数据全部直接写数据库，逐步把库填满

3. 图表数据流
   - 进入图表页或切周期时，先读数据库里这个“交易对 + 周期”的历史
   - 如果数据库里有，就先显示

- 需要新建数据库表、DAO、Repository，并把几个页面改成走数据库
- 但后面历史保留、增量更新、清缓存分项都会更稳

**User**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我继续把剩下 3 块补齐：数据库表、清缓存策略、页面改动范围。你看完如果也没问题，我就直接把设计文档改成 Room 版本。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

下面是 Room 方案的剩余设计。

**1. 表设计**
我建议最少拆成 5 张表，这样职责最清楚：

1. `kline_history`
   - 存每个交易对、每个周期的历史 K 线
   - 主键用 `symbol + interval + open_time`
   - 用来支撑图表长期历史、增量补齐、切周期秒开

2. `trade_history`
   - 存历史成交/平仓记录
   - 主键优先用 `deal_ticket`
   - 用来支撑历史交易长期保留、账户页历史列表

3. `position_snapshot`
   - 存当前持仓快照
   - 每次账户刷新时整批覆盖当前最新状态
   - 用来支撑账户页当前持仓、悬浮窗分产品盈亏

4. `pending_order_snapshot`
   - 存当前挂单快照
   - 每次账户刷新时整批覆盖
   - 用来支撑账户页挂单展示

5. `account_snapshot_meta`
   - 存账户摘要，比如更新时间、净值、保证金、统计指标
   - 只保留最新一份
   - 用来支撑账户页顶部摘要和悬浮窗连接附属信息

这样拆的好处是：历史数据和“当前状态”分开，后面不容易互相污染。

**2. 清缓存策略**
设置页我建议拆成 3 个独立动作：

1. 清除历史行情数据
   - 只删 `kline_history`

2. 清除历史交易数据
   - 只删 `trade_history`

3. 清除运行时缓存
   - 删当前快照类数据和临时缓存
   - 包括 `position_snapshot`、`pending_order_snapshot`、`account_snapshot_meta`，以及原来的临时内存/文件缓存

这样做的结果是：
- 你要保留历史，但想清掉“当前脏状态”时可以单独清
- 你要节省空间时，也可以只删历史行情或历史交易
- 不会再出现“一键全清后历史全没了”

**3. 页面改动范围**
1. 图表页
   - 改成先读 `kline_history`
   - 切页、切周期、启动时都统一走“先本地、后补最新”
   - 右侧留白改成绘图区 `1/7`

2. 账户页
   - 网关返回后先写数据库，再刷新界面
   - 顶部总盈亏改成红绿和更大字号
   - 历史交易从 `trade_history` 读，不再依赖临时内存拼接

3. 悬浮窗
   - 不再只看 BTC/XAU
   - 改成读 `position_snapshot`，按产品聚合盈亏
   - 删除“是否监控”，只保留连接状态

4. 监控页
   - 删除“是否开始监控”按钮
   - 服务默认监控
   - 页面只显示状态，不再承担开关职责

如果这三块你也确认没问题，我下一步就把设计文档改写成 Room 版本，然后发你文档路径让你过目。  
这次用了 `using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。

**OpenAI Codex**

设置页我这边会保持现在的一个“清理缓存数据”入口，但点进去后改成 3 个选项：历史行情、历史交易、运行时缓存。这样改动小，而且符合你要的“分开清理”。

# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><skills_instructions>

Use when Codex needs to create a new local plugin, add optional plugin structure, or generate or update repo-root `.agents/plugins/marketplace.json` entries for plugin ordering and availability metadata. ### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

---


**User**

另外还有一个问题是，目前的MT5 这条链路消耗大，但是我理解MT5主要返回的是持仓数据、挂单数据和历史订单。我理解的对不对？那么是否可以只实时推送持仓数据的变动，而挂单数据、历史订单只有在出现变化的时候在推送呢？这样做会不会大幅减少数据流量消耗？
之后，全面优化减少服务器向外发送的流量，以及手机APP的流量消耗的方案。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这次我先按 `using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming` 这三个 skill 来做：先读取项目上下文和当前链路实现，再判断你对 MT5 数据结构的理解是否准确，最后给出一套“先做什么、为什么能省流量”的完整方案。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我先看一下 MT5 网关现在到底在传什么、哪些接口已经做了摘要化，这样给你的结论会更准确，也能直接判断“只推持仓变化”到底能省多少。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经确认了一个关键点：你现在的 MT5 链路里，不只是“持仓、挂单、历史订单”，还包含账户摘要和历史曲线，所以真正的大头往往不是单条持仓本身，而是“反复把整包快照全量拉回来”。我再把具体字段和现有客户端拉取策略对上。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现在可以比较明确地说：你的判断方向是对的，但还差一层。真正该优化的不是“MT5 有没有很多种数据”，而是“App 现在是不是还在重复拿整份大包”。我再补一组关键频次参数，这样能把节流方案排出优先级。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经把链路确认完了。结论先提前说一句：这件事能明显降流量，而且最该做的是“把 MT5 数据拆成几条小链路”，而不是继续让 App 在很多场景下拿 `range=all` 的整包数据。下面我把依据和推荐方案整理成一套可执行的顺序。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

对，你的理解大方向是对的，但还不完整。

现在这条 MT5 链路返回的不只是“持仓、挂单、历史订单”，还包括账户摘要、统计指标、权益曲线这些内容。代码里完整快照接口会返回 `overviewMetrics / statsMetrics / curvePoints / positions / pendingOrders / trades`，可以在 [server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py#L787)、[server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py#L1251) 看到；后台现在默认 5 秒拉一次摘要，在 [AppConstants.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/constants/AppConstants.java#L74) 和 [AccountStatsPreloadManager.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsPreloadManager.java#L109) 可以看到。

所以，是否能明显省流量？答案是：能，而且通常会很明显。

按你前面贴出来的样本看：
- 当前持仓只有 `6` 条
- 挂单只有 `1` 条
- 历史成交有 `1046` 条
- 曲线点有 `2101` 个

这说明真正大的不是“实时持仓”，而是“历史成交 + 曲线 + 反复整包回传”。  
所以把策略改成：

- 持仓：实时推变动
- 挂单：只有变化时再推
- 历史订单：只有新增或变化时再推

这会明显减少流量。  
如果再把“曲线全量”也改成“只追加新点”，流量还能再降一大截。

**最推荐的全面优化方案**

1. 后台只保留一个“轻实时小接口”
内容只放：
- 账户关键数字
- 当前持仓
- 分产品盈亏
- 连接状态

不要带：
- 历史订单列表
- 挂单明细全量
- 全部曲线点

这样悬浮窗和后台常驻时，拿到的就是最小必要数据。

2. 挂单和历史订单拆成独立增量接口
不要再跟主快照绑一起。
改成：
- `pendingOrders`：只在有新增、撤单、修改时返回变化
- `trades`：只返回“上次之后新增的成交”

这样就不会因为持仓变一下，把挂单和历史订单整包再发一遍。

3. 权益曲线改成“追加模式”
不要每次发完整 `curvePoints`。
改成：
- 第一次进账户页时拉一次历史
- 后面只追加新点
- 本地 Room 永久保存

这条通常也是大头之一。

4. 按页面场景分流
- 后台常驻/悬浮窗：只拉“轻实时小接口”
- 账户页前台：拉摘要 + 增量成交 + 增量挂单 + 曲线追加
- 图表页前台：只补它当前真的要用的数据，不顺手把 MT5 全历史也拉回来

5. 轮询频率再压一档
你现在账户链路默认 5 秒一次，即一天 `17280` 次请求。  
建议改成：
- 后台常驻：10 到 15 秒
- 悬浮窗打开：3 到 5 秒
- 账户页前台：5 秒
- 连续多次无变化：自动退避到 15 到 30 秒

6. 保留现在已有的 `delta`，但进一步细分同步键
你现在客户端已经支持 `since + delta=1`，在 [Mt5BridgeGatewayClient.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/Mt5BridgeGatewayClient.java#L152) 和 [server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py#L981) 能看到。  
下一步不是推翻它，而是把它从“一个大快照的增量”升级成“多条小接口各自增量”。

**一句话结论**

只实时推持仓，挂单和历史订单只在变化时推，这个思路是对的，而且会明显减少流量；但如果想把流量真正压到低位，关键还要把“历史订单全量”和“曲线全量”从主链路里拆出去。

如果按收益排序，我建议下一步就做这一套顺序：
1. 后台接口只保留持仓摘要
2. 历史订单改增量
3. 挂单改增量
4. 曲线改追加
5. 再调低轮询频率

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。  
如果后面你想把这套节流改造成完整执行清单，也可以用 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai) 做更长链路的整理。

**OpenAI Codex**

测试已经补上了。现在先故意跑一遍，让它按预期失败，这样后面的实现才算真的有被这些测试约束住。

**OpenAI Codex**

已按这个顺序把节流优化落到代码里了。

这次的核心变化是：
- 网关新增了轻实时和分项增量接口，在 [server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py) 里把 MT5 数据拆成了 `/v1/live`、`/v1/pending`、`/v1/trades`、`/v1/curve`。现在后台只需要拿“账户关键指标 + 当前持仓”，挂单、历史成交、曲线改成各自按变化同步。

- 后台预加载在 [AccountStatsPreloadManager.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsPreloadManager.java) 改成走 `fetchLive()`，并把后台轮询间隔放慢到原来的 2 倍；持久层在 [AccountStorageRepository.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/data/local/db/repository/AccountStorageRepository.java) 新增了 `persistLiveSnapshot()`，只刷新摘要和持仓，不会把挂单和历史交易清空。

**OpenAI Codex**

已经把部署物准备好了：

- 服务器上传包：[`windows_server_bundle_2026-03-31.zip`](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle_2026-03-31.zip)
- 新 APK：[`app-debug.apk`](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk)

我还核对过一次，部署包里的网关代码和当前仓库里的 [server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py) 哈希一致，说明上传包已经是最新版本。

**现在你在韩国服务器上这样做**

1. 把 [`windows_server_bundle_2026-03-31.zip`](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle_2026-03-31.zip) 上传到服务器。
2. 服务器里先停掉当前手动运行的网关窗口。如果你之前是 `.\start_gateway.ps1` 开着的，直接在那个窗口里 `Ctrl+C`。
3. 管理员 PowerShell 执行：

```powershell
$zip = "C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\windows_server_bundle_2026-03-31.zip"
$temp = "C:\mt5_bundle_update"
$target = "C:\mt5_bundle"

if (Test-Path $temp) { Remove-Item -LiteralPath $temp -Recurse -Force }
Expand-Archive -LiteralPath $zip -DestinationPath $temp -Force
Copy-Item -LiteralPath "$temp\windows_server_bundle\*" -Destination $target -Recurse -Force
```

4. 重新启动网关：

```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway
.\start_gateway.ps1
```

5. 本机先验证新接口：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/health
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/live?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/pending?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/trades?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/curve?range=all
```

6. 如果都能返回数据，再重新注册并触发自启任务：

```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle
.\windows\02_register_startup_task.ps1 -BundleRoot 'C:\mt5_bundle' -Force
.\windows\03_run_healthcheck.ps1
```

7. 再测公网：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/live?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/pending?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/trades?range=all
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/v1/curve?range=all
```

**手机这边**

如果你电脑装了 `adb`，直接执行：

```powershell
adb install -r E:\Github\BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK\app\build\outputs\apk\debug\app-debug.apk
```

如果没有 `adb`，就把这个 APK 安装到手机：
[`app-debug.apk`](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk)

**你做完后，把这 5 条命令的返回结果发我就行**

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://150.109.252.239/mt5/health
```

现在你直接上传这个文件夹到服务器：
[`deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle`](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle)

我已完成并验证的内容：
- `gradle.properties` 已改成 `43.155.214.62`
- 新 APK 已重新构建，时间是 `2026/3/31 00:17:31`
- 生成的 `BuildConfig` 里 3 个地址都已经是 `43.155.214.62`
- 部署文档和服务器包内说明也都改成新 IP
- 服务器上传包仍是文件夹形式：[windows_server_bundle](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/deploy/tencent/windows_server_bundle)

- `C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway`
- `C:\mt5_bundle\windows`

```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway
.\start_gateway.ps1
```

如果你愿意，我下一条就直接继续带你做“把这个文件夹覆盖到服务器 + 重启网关 + 验证 5 个接口”的具体命令。
